<tr>\n        <td class="hlist noprint nowrap" colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top: 1px solid #aaa; padding-top: 3px;">\n         <a href="/wiki/Pacific_hurricane" title="Pacific hurricane">\n          Pacific hurricane seasons\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n          2015\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/2016_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2016 Pacific hurricane season">\n          2016\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <b>\n          2017\n         </b>\n         ,\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Pacific_hurricane" title="Pacific hurricane">\n           2018\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ,\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Pacific_hurricane" title="Pacific hurricane">\n           2019\n          </a>\n         </i>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <b>\n        2017 Pacific hurricane season\n       </b>\n       is an ongoing event in the annual cycle of tropical cyclone formation, in which tropical cyclones form in the northeastern Pacific Ocean. The season officially started on May\xc2\xa015 in the eastern Pacific, and on June\xc2\xa01 in the central Pacific; they will both end on November\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-season_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-season-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These dates conventionally delimit the period of each year when most tropical cyclones form in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pacific_hurricane" title="Pacific hurricane">\n        basin\n       </a>\n       . However, the formation of tropical cyclones is possible at any time of the year. This was demonstrated when the first storm, Tropical Storm Adrian, was\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        named\n       </a>\n       on May\xc2\xa010, and became the earliest-known tropical storm in the East Pacific since the advent of satellite imagery. Thus far, the season has seen near-average activity in terms of\n       <a href="/wiki/Accumulated_cyclone_energy" title="Accumulated cyclone energy">\n        ACE\n       </a>\n       , in stark contrast to the extremely active seasons in\n       <a href="/wiki/2014_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2014 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2014\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2015\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/2016_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2016 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2016\n       </a>\n       . For the third year in a row, the season featured above average activity in July, with the ACE value being the fifth highest for the month. However, as of November 7, no tropical cyclones have formed in the Central Pacific. If the season ends without a tropical cyclone forming there, it would be the first time since\n       <a href="/wiki/2012_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2012 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2012\n       </a>\n       that this happened. Despite being very active, the season featured the weakest storms since the\n       <a href="/wiki/2013_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2013 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2013 season\n       </a>\n       , with the strongest storm only dropping to 947 millibars.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Beginning this year, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       has the option to issue advisories, and thus allow watches and warnings to be issued, on disturbances that are not yet tropical cyclones but have a high chance to become one, and are expected to bring tropical storm or hurricane conditions to landmasses within 48\xc2\xa0hours. Such systems are classified as "Potential Tropical Cyclones". Advisories on these storms contain the same content, including track forecasts and cyclone watches and warnings, as advisories on active tropical cyclones.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This was first demonstrated on August\xc2\xa029 with the designation of Potential Tropical Cyclone Fourteen-E\xe2\x80\x94which later developed into\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Lidia_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Lidia (2017)">\n        Tropical Storm Lidia\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94south-southeast of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline"       </th>\n        <th>\n         Source\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Named\n         <br/>\n         storms\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Hurricanes\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Major\n         <br/>\n         hurricanes\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Ref\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         May 25, 2017\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/National_Oceanic_and_Atmospheric_Administration" title="National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration">\n          NOAA\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         14\xe2\x80\x9320\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6\xe2\x80\x9311\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         3\xe2\x80\x937\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NOAA_5-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-NOAA-5">\n           [5]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         May 29, 2017\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Servicio_Meteorol%C3%B3gico_Nacional_(Mexico)" title="Servicio Meteorol\xc3\xb3gico Nacional (Mexico)">\n          SMN\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         16\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         10\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SMN_6-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-SMN-6">\n           [6]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Area\n        </th>\n EPAC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         18\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         9\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         4\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          Actual activity\n         </b>\n         :\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         CPAC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <b>\n          Actual activity\n         </b>\n         :\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         18\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         9\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         4\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On May\xc2\xa025, 2017, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Oceanic_and_Atmospheric_Administration" title="National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration">\n        National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration\n       </a>\n       released its annual forecast, predicting a 80% chance of a near- to above-average season in both the Eastern and Central Pacific basins, with a total of 14\xe2\x80\x9320 named storms, 6\xe2\x80\x9311 hurricanes, and 3\xe2\x80\x937 major hurricanes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [nb 1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NOAA_5-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NOAA-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During May 28, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Servicio_Meteorol%C3%B3gico_Nacional" title="Servicio Meteorol\xc3\xb3gico Nacional">\n        Servicio Meteorol\xc3\xb3gico Nacional\n       </a>\n       (SMN) issued its first forecast for the season, predicting a total of 16 named storms, 10 hurricanes and 6 major hurricanes to develop.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SMN_6-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SMN-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Seasonal_summary">\n        Seasonal summary\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Seasonal summary">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_the_2017_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="Timeline of the 2017 Pacific hurricane season">\n        Timeline of the 2017 Pacific hurricane season\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <center>\n       <div class="timeline-wrapper">\n        <map id="timeline_6ab5d95b9d4e607e5cca8e1426114d09" name="timeline_6ab5d95b9d4e607e5cca8e1426114d09">\n         <area alt="Tropical Storm Lidia (2017)" coords="452,64,516,84" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Lidia_(2017)" shape="rect" title="Tropical Storm Lidia (2017)"/>\n         <area alt="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale" coords="602,198,761,218" href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" shape="rect" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale"/>\n        </map>\n        <img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/6ab5d95b9d4e607e5cca8e1426114d09.png" usemap="#timeline_6ab5d95b9d4e607e5cca8e1426114d09"/>\n       </div>\n      </center>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Accumulated_Cyclone_Energy" title="Accumulated Cyclone Energy">\n        Accumulated Cyclone Energy\n       </a>\n       (ACE) for the 2017 Pacific hurricane season, as of Selma\'s final advisory, is 98.0225\xc2\xa0units (97.09\xc2\xa0units from the East Pacific and 0.9325\xc2\xa0units from the Central Pacific).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [nb 2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Although the East Pacific hurricane season does not officially begin until May\xc2\xa015, activity began several days prior with the formation of a tropical depression on May\xc2\xa09. This marked the earliest formation of a tropical cyclone in the basin, surpassing\n       <a href="/wiki/1990_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Alma" title="1990 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1990\'s Hurricane Alma\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Adrianrecord_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Adrianrecord-9">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It intensified into Tropical Storm Adrian a few hours later, marking the earliest formation of a named storm on record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Near normal activity occurred in June, with Tropical Storm Calvin formed on June 11, and Hurricane Dora on June 25.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       For the third year in a row, July featured above average activity, with the fifth highest ACE value for that month on record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">\n        This total was attributed to long lived hurricanes Eugene, Fernanda, Hilary and Irwin. August saw significantly less activity, with only three storms forming in the month; however it featured Hurricane Kenneth, the third major hurricane of the season. September featured four storms, including Hurricane Otis, which became the fourth major hurricane of the season. Activity slowed considerably during the end of the month, only two storms formed after September 23, both of which did not attain hurricane intensity. After Ramon dissipated on October 5, activity ceased with no further storms forming until Tropical Storm Selma, which formed in late October.\n       </span>\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2017)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Systems">\n        Systems\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Systems">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Adrian">\n        Tropical Storm Adrian\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Adrian">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Adrian 2017-05-09 1912Z.jpg" data-file-height="1302" data-file-width="1002" height="195" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg/150px-Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg/225px-Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg/300px-Adrian_2017-05-09_1912Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Adrian_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Adrian 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Adrian_2017_track.png/150px-Adrian_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Adrian_2017_track.png/225px-Adrian_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Adrian_2017_track.png/300px-Adrian_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         May 9\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 May 11\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1004\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_off-season_Pacific_hurricanes" title="List of off-season Pacific hurricanes">\n        List of off-season Pacific hurricanes\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On May\xc2\xa05, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       (NHC) indicated that an\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">\n        area of low pressure\n       </a>\n       was forecast to form south of Mexico over subsequent days, with the possibility of tropical cyclone development thereafter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A broad\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_circulation" title="Atmospheric circulation">\n        cyclonic circulation\n       </a>\n       began to develop as expected late on May\xc2\xa07,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       gradually organizing into the season\'s first tropical depression by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on May\xc2\xa09.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Upon formation, at which point it was located about 545\xc2\xa0mi (875\xc2\xa0km) south-southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Salina_Cruz" title="Salina Cruz">\n        Salina Cruz, Mexico\n       </a>\n       , the depression became the earliest-forming East Pacific tropical cyclone (east of 140\xc2\xb0W) on record. The previous record was held by\n       <a href="/wiki/1990_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Alma" title="1990 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1990\'s Hurricane Alma\n       </a>\n       , which formed on May 12.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Adrianrecord_9-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Adrianrecord-9">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The depression intensified into Tropical Storm Adrian six hours later, the earliest-known formation of a named storm in eastern Pacific proper since the advent of the satellite era.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Initially, forecasts expected the small storm to intensify into a powerful hurricane. Shortly after reaching peak intensity early on May 10, an unexpected increase in mid-level\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       caused Adrian to quickly weaken back to a tropical depression by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on May 11.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on the next day, Adrian degenerated into a remnant low.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Beatriz">\n        Tropical Storm Beatriz\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Beatriz">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Beatriz 2017-06-01 1710Z.jpg" data-file-height="7800" data-file-width="6000" height="195" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg/150px-Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg/225px-Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg/300px-Beatriz_2017-06-01_1710Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beatriz_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Beatriz 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Beatriz_2017_track.png/150px-Beatriz_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Beatriz_2017_track.png/225px-Beatriz_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Beatriz_2017_track.png/300px-Beatriz_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         May 31\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 June 2\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1001\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical wave emerged off the western coast of Africa on May\xc2\xa018 and entered the East Pacific about a week later, where steady organization led to the formation of a tropical depression around 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on May\xc2\xa031. Embedded within southwesterly flow around a large upper-level trough across northern Mexico, the depression moved steadily northeast in a favorable environment, and it intensified into Tropical Storm Beatriz by 06:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa01. After attaining peak winds of 45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h), the system made landfall around 00:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa02 about 25\xc2\xa0miles (40\xc2\xa0km) west of\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_%C3%81ngel" title="Puerto \xc3\x81ngel">\n        Puerto \xc3\x81ngel\n       </a>\n       . The mountainous terrain of Mexico quickly disrupted Beatriz, and it ultimately dissipated twelve hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Btcr_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Btcr-19">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the state of\n       <a href="/wiki/Oaxaca" title="Oaxaca">\n        Oaxaca\n       </a>\n       , flights out of\n       <a href="/wiki/Bah%C3%ADas_de_Huatulco_International_Airport" title="Bah\xc3\xadas de Huatulco International Airport">\n        Bah\xc3\xadas de Huatulco International Airport\n       </a>\n       were cancelled, and schools were closed until at least June\xc2\xa03. Dozens of roads were rendered impassable due to mudslides and flooding; numerous locales received over 4\xc2\xa0in (102\xc2\xa0mm) of rain, with a storm total of 19.07\xc2\xa0in (484.4\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Huatulco" title="Huatulco">\n        Huatulco\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Btcr_19-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Btcr-19">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Numerous\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landslides" title="Landslides">\n        landslides\n       </a>\n       caused significant disruption across the state, especially by blocking\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Federal_Highway_200" title="Mexican Federal Highway 200">\n        Federal Highway 200\n       </a>\n       at many areas. A landslide in\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Marcial_Ozolotepec" title="San Marcial Ozolotepec">\n        San Marcial Ozolotepec\n       </a>\n       killed two girls and buried several houses, while another in\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Carlos_Yautepec" title="San Carlos Yautepec">\n        San Carlos Yautepec\n       </a>\n       killed a woman.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of June 4, a total of seven people have been killed\xe2\x80\x94five in Oaxaca and two in\n       <a href="/wiki/Tehuantepec" title="Tehuantepec">\n        Tehuantepec\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Less than two weeks after Beatriz, Tropical Storm Calvin affected similar areas of Mexico and inflicted additional damage. Combined damage from the two systems reached at least 70\xc2\xa0million pesos (US$3.9\xc2\xa0million) in Oaxaca.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Calvin">\n        Tropical Storm Calvin\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Calvin">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Calvin 2017-06-12 2000Z.jpg" data-file-height="7200" data-file-width="5600" height="193" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg/150px-Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg/225px-Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg/300px-Calvin_2017-06-12_2000Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Calvin_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Calvin 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Calvin_2017_track.png/150px-Calvin_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Calvin_2017_track.png/225px-Calvin_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Calvin_2017_track.png/300px-Calvin_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         June 11\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 June 13\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1004\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       In the second week of June, the NHC forecast the development of a broad area of low pressure a few hundred miles south of Mexico over the next several days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This prediction came to fruition on June\xc2\xa09,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the fledgling disturbance steadily organized into a tropical depression by 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa011 while located about 150\xc2\xa0mi (240\xc2\xa0km) south-southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Salina_Cruz" title="Salina Cruz">\n        Salina Cruz\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ctcr_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ctcr-25">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was slow to organize initially amid moderate easterly wind shear as it drifted northwestwards;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       by 18:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa012, however, the tropical depression intensified into Tropical Storm Calvin.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ctcr_25-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ctcr-25">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Intensifying slightly to reach winds of 45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ctcr_25-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ctcr-25">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Calvin made\n       <a href="/wiki/Landfall" title="Landfall">\n        landfall\n       </a>\n       halfway between Salina Cruz and Puerto \xc3\x81ngel, near Paja Blanca, around 00:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa013.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Just 12\xc2\xa0hours later, Calvin dissipated into a remnant low.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ctcr_25-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ctcr-25">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The remnants of the storm caused heavy rainfall and some flooding in the area,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       however no fatalities were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ctcr_25-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ctcr-25">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Dora">\n        Hurricane Dora\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Hurricane Dora">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Dora 2017-06-26 2020Z.jpg" data-file-height="10859" data-file-width="8021" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg/150px-Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg/225px-Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg/300px-Dora_2017-06-26_2020Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dora_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Dora 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Dora_2017_track.png/150px-Dora_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Dora_2017_track.png/225px-Dora_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Dora_2017_track.png/300px-Dora_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         June 25\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 June 28\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         981\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On June\xc2\xa021, the NHC began monitoring a broad area of low pressure south of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Tehuantepec" title="Gulf of Tehuantepec">\n        Gulf of Tehuantepec\n       </a>\n       for possible tropical cyclogenesis.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance organized into a tropical depression by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on June\xc2\xa025,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and became a tropical storm six hours later, receiving the name\n       <i>\n        Dora\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Progressing in a west-northwesterly direction at a steady speed, the storm began a 30-hour period of rapid intensification and became the first hurricane of the season at 09:00 UTC on June 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With impressive upper-level outflow and an\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       apparent on satellite imagery,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the storm attained peak winds of 90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h) by late on June\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Dora maintained its intensity for a number of hours before beginning to rapidly weaken over cooler sea surface temperatures and in an environment of drier air.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm later degenerated into a remnant low early on June 28, after all of the storm\'s deep convection had dissipated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The outer bands of Dora brought heavy rains to\n       <a href="/wiki/Guerrero" title="Guerrero">\n        Guerrero\n       </a>\n       , resulting in flash floods that inundated 20\xc2\xa0homes. Overall damage was minor, however.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Eugene">\n        Hurricane Eugene\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Hurricane Eugene">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">\n         Category 3\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Eugene 2017-07-09 1815Z.jpg" data-file-height="6679" data-file-width="5066" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg/150px-Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg/225px-Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg/300px-Eugene_2017-07-09_1815Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eugene_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Eugene 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Eugene_2017_track.png/150px-Eugene_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Eugene_2017_track.png/225px-Eugene_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Eugene_2017_track.png/300px-Eugene_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 7\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 12\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         966\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Eugene developed from a disturbance located 765\xc2\xa0mi (1,230\xc2\xa0km) south of the southern tip of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       on July 7.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On the following day, Eugene underwent a period of\n       <a href="/wiki/Rapid_intensification" title="Rapid intensification">\n        rapid intensification\n       </a>\n       ; in an 18-hour period starting at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa08, Eugene intensified from a tropical storm with 70\xc2\xa0mph (110\xc2\xa0km/h) winds to a Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane with 115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h) winds, making it the first major hurricane of the season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, by 12 hours later, the entrainment of dry air caused Eugene to weaken to a Category\xc2\xa02 hurricane,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and due to traveling over cooler waters, Eugene weakened to a tropical storm on the following day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the coverage of deep convection steadily dwindled, Eugene fell to tropical depression intensity around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa012 and degenerated to a remnant low six hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Dangerous\n       <a href="/wiki/Rip_current" title="Rip current">\n        rip currents\n       </a>\n       combined with swells of 4 to 8\xc2\xa0ft (1.2 to 2.4\xc2\xa0m) across southern California resulted in hundreds of rescues. On July\xc2\xa010 alone, lifeguards in\n       <a href="/wiki/Huntington_Beach,_California" title="Huntington Beach, California">\n        Huntington Beach\n       </a>\n       made 200\xc2\xa0rescues while 600 were made in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_County" title="Los Angeles County">\n        Los Angeles County\n       </a>\n       ; lifeguards also responded to 700\xc2\xa0medical emergencies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">\n        <a href="#cite_note-45">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Fernanda">\n        Hurricane Fernanda\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Hurricane Fernanda">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Fernanda 2017-07-14 2135Z.jpg" data-file-height="7757" data-file-width="5796" height="201" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg/150px-Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg/225px-Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg/300px-Fernanda_2017-07-14_2135Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fernanda_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Fernanda 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Fernanda_2017_track.png/150px-Fernanda_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Fernanda_2017_track.png/225px-Fernanda_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Fernanda_2017_track.png/300px-Fernanda_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 12\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 22\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         145\xc2\xa0mph (230\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         947\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Late on July\xc2\xa010, the NHC began monitoring a broad area of low pressure several hundred miles southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Manzanillo,_Colima" title="Manzanillo, Colima">\n        Manzanillo\n       </a>\n       . Contrary to predictions of gradual development,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the disturbance rapidly organized into a tropical depression by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa012,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and further strengthened to become Tropical Storm Fernanda around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The nascent cyclone initially battled moderate northeasterly wind shear, with its low-level circulation displaced to the northeastern edge of the deep convection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This period of unfavorable upper-level winds was short-lived, and soon afterwards Fernanda commenced a period of\n       <a href="/wiki/Rapid_intensification" title="Rapid intensification">\n        rapid intensification\n       </a>\n       , intensifying into a hurricane at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa013.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n        <a href="#cite_note-50">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A well-defined eye formed within a growing\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_dense_overcast" title="Central dense overcast">\n        central dense overcast\n       </a>\n       , and Fernanda further intensified into a major hurricane early on July 14.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Only six hours later, the system was upgraded to a Category 4 hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At 10.9\xc2\xb0N, Fernanda became the second strongest hurricane to occur at such a low latitude in the Eastern Pacific, only behind\n       <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Olaf" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2015\'s Hurricane Olaf\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n        <a href="#cite_note-53">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       With expansive upper-level outflow and spiral bands, a distinct eye, and a symmetric central dense overcast, Fernanda attained peak winds of 145\xc2\xa0mph (230\xc2\xa0km/h) around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa015.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n        <a href="#cite_note-54">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A series of microwave passes around that time began to indicate the formation of a secondary eyewall that halted the cyclone\'s development as it tracked west-northwest to northwest.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The eyewall replacement cycle concluded early on July\xc2\xa016, allowing Fernanda to remain a powerful hurricane amid favorable environmental conditions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56">\n        <a href="#cite_note-56">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By late on July\xc2\xa018, however, cooler ocean temperatures and a more stable environment prompted the storm\'s weakening trend.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">\n        <a href="#cite_note-57">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Fernanda fell below hurricane intensity shortly before entering the Central Pacific as it succumbed to stronger southwesterly wind shear,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a href="#cite_note-58">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and after failing to produce sustained deep convection, degenerated to a remnant low about 500\xc2\xa0miles (805\xc2\xa0km) east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hilo,_Hawaii" title="Hilo, Hawaii">\n        Hilo, Hawaii\n       </a>\n       , by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa022.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n        <a href="#cite_note-59">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Greg">\n        Tropical Storm Greg\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Greg">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Greg 2017-07-21 1835Z.jpg" data-file-height="5665" data-file-width="4417" height="192" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg/150px-Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg/225px-Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg/300px-Greg_2017-07-21_1835Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Greg Pacific 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png/150px-Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png/225px-Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png/300px-Greg_Pacific_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 17\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 26\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         60\xc2\xa0mph (95\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1001\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On July\xc2\xa012, the NHC forecast the formation of a broad area of low pressure south of Mexico over subsequent days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">\n        <a href="#cite_note-60">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance formed two days later and slowly organized into a tropical depression by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa017.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">\n        <a href="#cite_note-61">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone battled strong west-northwesterly wind shear after formation, intensifying into Tropical Storm Greg by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa018 as deep convection burst near the center, but remained steady state for several days thereafter despite continued predictions of intensification.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">\n        <a href="#cite_note-64">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ultimately, given global models\' poor handling of the environment, NHC lowered their intensity forecast for Greg.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone continued west for the remainder of its life and maintained a similar convective structure, with intermittent bursts of deep convection near the center.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Approaching the Central Pacific, Greg\'s low-level circulation became increasingly difficult to locate as it moved into a cooler, drier environment intertwined by increasing southerly wind shear, and the system weakened to a tropical depression around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa025.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">\n        <a href="#cite_note-67">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It degenerated to a remnant low 24 hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">\n        <a href="#cite_note-68">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Eight-E">\n        Tropical Depression Eight-E\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Eight-E">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="08E 2017-07-18 1805Z.jpg" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1084" height="190" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg/150px-08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg/225px-08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg/300px-08E_2017-07-18_1805Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:08E_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="08E 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/08E_2017_track.png/150px-08E_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/08E_2017_track.png/225px-08E_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/08E_2017_track.png/300px-08E_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 18\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 20\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1007\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A low-pressure trough began producing disorganized convection over the waters of the Pacific Ocean, well to the south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       , on July\xc2\xa014.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite only marginally conducive environmental conditions, the disturbance began to show signs of organization two days later,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and it attained tropical depression status by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa018.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">\n        <a href="#cite_note-71">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Strong west-northwesterly\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       confined the storm\'s intermittent bursts of convection well to the southwest of its low-level circulation, and the depression consequently failed to produce winds above 35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system\'s center later degenerated into a low-pressure trough within the\n       <a href="/wiki/Intertropical_Convergence_Zone" title="Intertropical Convergence Zone">\n        Intertropical Convergence Zone\n       </a>\n       , prompting the NHC to discontinue advisories at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa020.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Hilary">\n        Hurricane Hilary\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Hurricane Hilary">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Hilary 2017-07-25 2015Z.jpg" data-file-height="6393" data-file-width="5140" height="187" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg/150px-Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg/225px-Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg/300px-Hilary_2017-07-25_2015Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hilary_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Hilary 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Hilary_2017_track.png/150px-Hilary_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Hilary_2017_track.png/225px-Hilary_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Hilary_2017_track.png/300px-Hilary_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 21\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 31\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         972\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Part of an exceptionally active July, the NHC began highlighting the far eastern reaches of the Pacific basin on July\xc2\xa019 for tropical development in later days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daniel_P._Brown_74-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Daniel_P._Brown-74">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A large area of disturbed weather progressed westward across\n       <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica" title="Costa Rica">\n        Costa Rica\n       </a>\n       later that day,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       steadily organizing into a tropical depression by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa021.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone failed to organize immediately after formation, and its low-level center migrated to the southern extent of associated convection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa023, though, better defined banding features and a more organized convective structure led the NHC to designate the system as Tropical Storm Hilary.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over the coming hours, the cyclone\'s convective structure evolved into a small central dense overcast while hints of an eye became apparent;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in accordance with satellite estimates, Hilary was upgraded to a hurricane at 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa024.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A moist environment and warm ocean waters propelled Hilary to its peak as a Category\xc2\xa02 hurricane with winds of 105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h) 24 hours later, at which time its core was most symmetric.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After maintaining its intensity, the hurricane began to weaken late on July\xc2\xa026 as northerly wind shear increased.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">\n        <a href="#cite_note-82">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It fell back to tropical storm intensity around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa027 and ultimately degenerated to a remnant low four days later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n        <a href="#cite_note-83">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Irwin">\n        Hurricane Irwin\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Hurricane Irwin">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Irwin 2017-07-25 2120Z.jpg" data-file-height="10039" data-file-width="8093" height="186" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg/150px-Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg/225px-Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg/300px-Irwin_2017-07-25_2120Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irwin_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Irwin 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1907" data-file-width="3000" height="95" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Irwin_2017_track.png/150px-Irwin_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Irwin_2017_track.png/225px-Irwin_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Irwin_2017_track.png/300px-Irwin_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 22\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 1\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         980\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On July\xc2\xa016, the NHC highlighted the expected formation of an area of low pressure south of Mexico later that week.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A tropical wave began producing disorganized cloudiness three days later,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daniel_P._Brown_74-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Daniel_P._Brown-74">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the broad system slowly organized into a tropical depression by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa022.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Its structure changed little after formation, impinged by strong wind shear; despite this, satellite wind data indicated the cyclone intensified into Tropical Storm Irwin by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa023.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over the next 24 hours, deep convection began to wrap around the center and a mid-level eye formed as environmental conditions improved;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa025, Irwin intensified into a hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although coolest cloudtops were located in the western semicircle of the system, a well-defined eye and convection in the eyewall propelled Irwin to its peak with winds of 90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h) late on July\xc2\xa025.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Almost immediately, outflow from nearby Hurricane Hilary increased wind shear over the system and caused it to begin weakening;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Irwin rapidly fell to tropical storm strength around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on July\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Contrary to projections of continued weakening, however, the storm\'s cloud pattern maintained or even improved over subsequent days as it passed over marginal ocean temperatures.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Finally, after losing its deep convection and being reduced to a swirl of low-level clouds, Irwin was declared a remnant low around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa01.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Eleven-E">\n        Tropical Depression Eleven-E\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Eleven-E">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="11E 2017-08-04 2015Z.jpg" data-file-height="6193" data-file-width="4577" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg/150px-11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg/225px-11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg/300px-11E_2017-08-04_2015Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:11E_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="11E 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/11E_2017_track.png/150px-11E_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/11E_2017_track.png/225px-11E_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/11E_2017_track.png/300px-11E_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 4\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 5\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1004\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On July\xc2\xa028, the NHC advertised the likely development of an area of low pressure well south of Mexico over subsequent days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An area of disorganized showers and thunderstorms associated with a tropical wave materialized three days later, but little change occurred thereafter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on August\xc2\xa03, a surface circulation formed in association with concentrating convection,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and this process led to the formation of a tropical depression by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC the next day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The newly formed cyclone did not intensify after designation, and its low- and mid-level circulations separated by over 265\xc2\xa0mi (425\xc2\xa0km) on August\xc2\xa05.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Falling short of the tropical cyclone criteria, the short-lived depression was declared a remnant low at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Jova">\n        Tropical Storm Jova\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Jova">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg">\n            <img alt="Jova 2017-08-11 Suomi NPP.jpg" data-file-height="2862" data-file-width="2161" height="199" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg/150px-Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg/225px-Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg/300px-Jova_2017-08-11_Suomi_NPP.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jova_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Jova 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Jova_2017_track.png/150px-Jova_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Jova_2017_track.png/225px-Jova_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Jova_2017_track.png/300px-Jova_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 12\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 14\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         40\xc2\xa0mph (65\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1003\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The NHC began monitoring a strong tropical wave over the eastern Caribbean on August\xc2\xa03.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The feature pushed westward, developing into\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Franklin" title="Hurricane Franklin">\n        Hurricane Franklin\n       </a>\n       before making landfall on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and attaining its peak as a Category\xc2\xa01 hurricane before making landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Vega_de_Alatorre" title="Vega de Alatorre">\n        Vega de Alatorre, Veracruz\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although its low-level circulation dissipated, the NHC in days prior noted the potential for Franklin\'s mid-level remnants to reform in the East Pacific.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n
