  </sup>\n       The remnants of Franklin induced a surface low off the coast of southwestern Mexico on August\xc2\xa011, and steady organization led to the formation of Tropical Storm Jova by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC the next day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On a westward course, Jova was plagued by strong wind shear from an area of high pressure over northwestern Mexico, with a very disorganized appearance on satellite.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After lacking sufficient organization to be declared a tropical cyclone, the storm was declared a remnant low around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa014.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Kenneth">\n        Hurricane Kenneth\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Hurricane Kenneth">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Kenneth 2017-08-20 2156Z.jpg" data-file-height="8771" data-file-width="6077" height="216" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg/150px-Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg/225px-Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg/300px-Kenneth_2017-08-20_2156Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kenneth_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Kenneth 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Kenneth_2017_track.png/150px-Kenneth_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Kenneth_2017_track.png/225px-Kenneth_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Kenneth_2017_track.png/300px-Kenneth_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 18\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 23\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         952\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On August\xc2\xa012, the NHC noted the potential for an area of low pressure to form well south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       during the following days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A large area of disturbed weather developed two days later as predicted;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       however, organization was slow to occur, and a tropical depression only formed four days later, around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa018.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The newly formed cyclone embarked on a west to west-northwest course, intensifying into Tropical Storm Kenneth early on August\xc2\xa019 and further into a hurricane by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa020.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite forecasts of only slight additional intensification,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Kenneth rapidly intensified, with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye feature\n       </a>\n       warming dramatically and the surrounding cloud tops cooling. The cyclone attained\n       <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       strength around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa021,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and six hours later reached its peak as a Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane with sustained winds of 130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Progressively cooler\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       and increasing\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       caused Kenneth to steadily weaken following the intensification trend, with its inner core eroding and low-level circulation becoming displaced.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa022, the storm weakened below hurricane strength.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The following day, at 21:00 UTC, Kenneth was declared post-tropical.\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Lidia">\n        Tropical Storm Lidia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Lidia">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Lidia 2017-08-31 2023Z.jpg" data-file-height="9706" data-file-width="6734" height="216" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg/150px-Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg/225px-Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg/300px-Lidia_2017-08-31_2023Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lidia_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Lidia 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Lidia_2017_track.png/150px-Lidia_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Lidia_2017_track.png/225px-Lidia_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Lidia_2017_track.png/300px-Lidia_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 31\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 3\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         65\xc2\xa0mph (100\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         987\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Lidia_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Lidia (2017)">\n        Tropical Storm Lidia (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On August 29, the NHC monitored a potential area of Tropical Cyclone development near the coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">\n        Baja California\n       </a>\n       with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Watch" title="Tropical Storm Watch">\n        Tropical Storm Watches\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Watch" title="Hurricane Watch">\n        Hurricane Watches\n       </a>\n       stretching from\n       <a href="/wiki/Todos_Santos,_Baja_California_Sur" title="Todos Santos, Baja California Sur">\n        Todos Santos\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Los_Barriles,_Baja_California_Sur" title="Los Barriles, Baja California Sur">\n        Los Barriles\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n        <a href="#cite_note-117">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">\n        The NHC initiated advisories on Tropical Storm Lidia at 00:00\n        <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n         UTC\n        </a>\n        on August 31 about 180\xc2\xa0mi (290\xc2\xa0km) south-southeast of the southern tip of the\n        <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n         Baja California Peninsula\n        </a>\n        . Favorable conditions allowed Lidia to intensify, and by 21:00 UTC on August 31, the storm peaked with\n        <a href="/wiki/Maximum_sustained_wind" title="Maximum sustained wind">\n         maximum sustained winds\n        </a>\n        of 65\xc2\xa0mph (100\xc2\xa0km/h) and a minimum\n        <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_pressure" title="Atmospheric pressure">\n         atmospheric pressure\n        </a>\n        of 987\n        <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n         mbar\n        </a>\n        (29.1\n        <a href="/wiki/Inch_of_mercury" title="Inch of mercury">\n         inHg\n        </a>\n        ). Around 12:00 UTC on the following day, Lidia made\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landfall_(meteorology)" title="Landfall (meteorology)">\n         landfall\n        </a>\n        near\n        <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Chale" title="Puerto Chale">\n         Puerto Chale\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Sur" title="Baja California Sur">\n         Baja California Sur\n        </a>\n        , at the same intensity. The cyclone weakened significantly while traversing the mountainous terrain of the\n        <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n         Baja California Peninsula\n        </a>\n        , and by early on September 2, deep convection was mainly limited to a few strong clusters near the center. Around that time, Lidia briefly moved offshore, before making another landfall near\n        <a href="/wiki/Punta_Abreojos" title="Punta Abreojos">\n         Punta Abreojos\n        </a>\n        a few hours later. By that time, Lidia had weakened steadily, and emerged over the Pacific Ocean on September 2. However, Lidia continued to weaken due to cold\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperatures" title="Sea surface temperatures">\n         sea surface temperatures\n        </a>\n        . After failing to produce deep convection for about 12\xe2\x80\x9315 hours, the NHC declared that Lidia had degenerated into a remnant low-pressure area at 09:00 UTC on September 2 about 40\xc2\xa0mi (65\xc2\xa0km/h) southwest of Punta Baja, Baja California.\n       </span>\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2017)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Otis">\n        Hurricane Otis\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Hurricane Otis">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">\n         Category 3\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Otis 2017-09-17 1915Z.jpg" data-file-height="7987" data-file-width="5754" height="208" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg/150px-Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg/225px-Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg/300px-Otis_2017-09-17_1915Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Otis_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Otis 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Otis_2017_track.png/150px-Otis_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Otis_2017_track.png/225px-Otis_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Otis_2017_track.png/300px-Otis_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 11\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 19\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         965\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On September 8,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katia_(2017)" title="Hurricane Katia (2017)">\n        Hurricane Katia\n       </a>\n       of the Atlantic made landfall on Mexico, dissipating on September 9. However, its mid-level circulation survived, and eventually spawned an area of low pressure off the coast of Mexico. On September 11, the system organized into Tropical Depression Fifteen-E. During the next several days, the depression slowly drifted westward, before strengthening into Tropical Storm Otis on September 16. While only marginal strengthening was forecast, Otis unexpectedly rapidly intensified into a Category 2 hurricane by 17:00 UTC on September 17, despite lower ocean temperatures, drier air, and increased wind shear.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Otis continued to intensify into a Category 3 major hurricane by 03:00 UTC on September 18, developing a well-defined eye with a diameter of 10 nautical miles (12\xc2\xa0mi; 19\xc2\xa0km).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 21:00 UTC on September 18, Otis had rapidly degenerated back into a tropical storm with maximum sustained winds of 40 knots (46\xc2\xa0mph; 74\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">\n        <a href="#cite_note-120">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Twelve hours after developing a well-defined eye, Otis started weakening at a remarkable rate, losing most of its deep convection from low ocean surface temperatures until it became a remnant low on September 19, due to a lack of convection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121">\n        <a href="#cite_note-121">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">\n        <a href="#cite_note-122">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Max">\n        Hurricane Max\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Hurricane Max">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Max 2017-09-14 1705Z.jpg" data-file-height="10753" data-file-width="7475" height="216" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg/150px-Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg/225px-Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg/300px-Max_2017-09-14_1705Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Max_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Max 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Max_2017_track.png/150px-Max_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Max_2017_track.png/225px-Max_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Max_2017_track.png/300px-Max_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 13\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 15\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         985\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On September\xc2\xa09, the NHC mentioned the possibility for an area of low pressure to form south of Mexico over later days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">\n        <a href="#cite_note-123">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A trough of low pressure materialized the next day,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       steadily organizing into a tropical depression near the southwestern coast of Mexico around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa013. Despite forecasts of little or no intensification,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">\n        <a href="#cite_note-125">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the newly formed cyclone intensified into Tropical Storm Max six hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Quick intensification ensued as the storm improved in structure and developed a well-defined eye, prompting the NHC to upgrade Max to a hurricane around 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa014.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After attaining peak winds of 85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the hurricane moved ashore the coastline of Guerrero at a slightly reduced strength around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The mountainous terrain of inland Mexico severely disrupted Max\'s circulation, causing it to degenerate by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa015.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In preparation for Max, about 788 people evacuated to temporary shelters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElManana_131-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ElManana-131">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Throughout Guerrero, over 1,500 homes were inundated by floodwaters or damaged by strong winds that ripped off roofs. Over 100 trees were downed, mudslides and sinkholes closed several roads (including\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Federal_Highway_200" title="Mexican Federal Highway 200">\n        Mexican Federal Highway 200\n       </a>\n       ), and telephone service was cut. At the height of the storm, 126,503\n       <a href="/wiki/Comisi%C3%B3n_Federal_de_Electricidad" title="Comisi\xc3\xb3n Federal de Electricidad">\n        Comisi\xc3\xb3n Federal de Electricidad\n       </a>\n       customers lost electricity. A bridge between\n       <a href="/wiki/Cruz_Grande" title="Cruz Grande">\n        Cruz Grande\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Copala,_Guerrero" title="Copala, Guerrero">\n        Copala\n       </a>\n       was severely damaged, and access to\n       <a href="/wiki/Juchit%C3%A1n_de_Zaragoza" title="Juchit\xc3\xa1n de Zaragoza">\n        Juchit\xc3\xa1n de Zaragoza\n       </a>\n       was severed due to a flooded highway. One of 17 rapidly-rising rivers swept away a residence and two neighbors who attempted to rescue the homeowner; one of the neighbors died, constituting one of two deaths attributed to the storm. At least 3,000 residents across five municipalities in Guerrero were stranded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElManana_131-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ElManana-131">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n        <a href="#cite_note-132">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Waves of 10\xe2\x80\x9316\xc2\xa0ft (3\xe2\x80\x935\xc2\xa0m) battered the coastline, where six ships were sunk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">\n        <a href="#cite_note-133">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Norma">\n        Hurricane Norma\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Hurricane Norma">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Norma 2017-09-15 2055Z.jpg" data-file-height="7823" data-file-width="5583" height="210" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg/150px-Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg/225px-Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg/300px-Norma_2017-09-15_2055Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Norma_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Norma 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Norma_2017_track.png/150px-Norma_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Norma_2017_track.png/225px-Norma_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Norma_2017_track.png/300px-Norma_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 14\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 20\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         75\xc2\xa0mph (120\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         985\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On September 10, the NHC started to monitor an area of low pressure well south of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manzanillo,_Mexico" title="Manzanillo, Mexico">\n        Manzanillo, Mexico\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">\n        <a href="#cite_note-134">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance gradually organized during the following days and by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa014 the system was noted to develop a well-defined center and spiral banding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135">\n        <a href="#cite_note-135">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This led to the formation of Tropical Storm Norma, skipping tropical depression status.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The newly formed tropical storm continued to intensify at a steady pace while it moved slowly northward, becoming a category 1 hurricane by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa016 and reaching winds of 75\xc2\xa0mph (120\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At this time warnings were being required for the southern portions of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       as Norma was forecast to become a major hurricane and make landfall in the area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, its broad circulation and the entrainment of dry air quickly became an impediment in doing so.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Norma then weakened back to a tropical storm at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC later that day while becoming stationary, though a developing ridge over\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </a>\n       began to move the storm slowly towards the north.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Norma maintained its intensity the next day and continued being slowly steered by the ridge towards a northwesterly to west-northwesterly path, all tropical storm warnings were discontinued as Norma started to shift its track more to the west.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">\n        <a href="#cite_note-141">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone continued weakening for several days as it slowly drifted to the west, until finally being declared a remnant low at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa020.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">\n        <a href="#cite_note-142">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Pilar">\n        Tropical Storm Pilar\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Pilar">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Pilar 2017-09-24 1740Z.jpg" data-file-height="5600" data-file-width="4400" height="191" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg/150px-Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg/225px-Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg/300px-Pilar_2017-09-24_1740Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pilar_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Pilar 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Pilar_2017_track.png/150px-Pilar_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Pilar_2017_track.png/225px-Pilar_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Pilar_2017_track.png/300px-Pilar_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 23\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 25\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       During the week of September 18, the NHC began monitoring a tropical wave,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">\n        <a href="#cite_note-143">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       as it spawned a broad area of low pressure located offshore of the southwestern coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">\n        <a href="#cite_note-144">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance lacked any significant organization until September 23 at around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC when the system was noted to developed surface winds of over 35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h) becoming Tropical Depression Eighteen-E.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">\n        <a href="#cite_note-145">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The depression organized into a tropical storm six hours later and was given the name\n       <i>\n        Pilar\n       </i>\n       , the sixteenth named storm of the annual Pacific hurricane season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Thereafter, despite having a disorganized appearance on satellite, Pilar\'s winds increased in strength, and it reached its peak with sustained winds of 45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September 24, Pilar continued to track north along the coast, with warnings being issued for the southwestern coast of Mexico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, early on September 25, these warnings were discontinued,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       as Tropical Storm Pilar showed signs of weakening mainly due to land interaction, and was reduced to a tropical depression before ultimately dissipating at around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC later that same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although Pilar did not make landfall as a tropical cyclone, heavy rainfall was reported in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puerto_Vallarta,_Mexico" title="Puerto Vallarta, Mexico">\n        Puerto Vallarta, Mexico\n       </a>\n       , northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Islas_Mar%C3%ADas" title="Islas Mar\xc3\xadas">\n        Islas Mar\xc3\xadas\n       </a>\n       and in other areas along the Mexican coastline.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">\n        <a href="#cite_note-151">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Ramon">\n        Tropical Storm Ramon\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Ramon">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ramon_2017-10-04_1945Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Ramon 2017-10-04 1945Z.jpg" data-file-height="8865" data-file-width="6721" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Ramon_2017-10-04_1945Z.jpg/150px-Ramon_2017-10-04_1945Z.jpg" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Ramon_2017-10-04_1945Z.jpg/300px-Ramon_2017-10-04_1945Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ramon_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Ramon 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Ramon_2017_track.png/150px-Ramon_2017_track.png" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Ramon_2017_track.png/300px-Ramon_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 4\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 5\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On October 3, the NHC noted a high chance of tropical development in an area of low pressure, to the south of Mexico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system increased in intensity and became Tropical Storm Ramon early on October 4, skipping tropical depression status.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to wind shear from a large anticyclone to its north, the storm did not intensify much further.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although it was forecast to linger over open waters as it moved westward, this did not occur and the system quickly grew disorganized.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">\n        <a href="#cite_note-155">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ramon weakened into a tropical depression later on the same day, having lasted as a tropical storm only for 18 hours.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">\n        <a href="#cite_note-156">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As it moved westward, Ramon continued to weaken, until it finally degenerated into a trough of low pressure on October 5, and the National Hurricane Center issued its last advisory on the degenerated system at 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC, on the same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">\n        <a href="#cite_note-157">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Selma">\n        Tropical Storm Selma\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Selma">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Selma 2017-10-28 1950Z.jpg" data-file-height="6385" data-file-width="4849" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg/150px-Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg/225px-Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg/300px-Selma_2017-10-28_1950Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 27\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 28\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         40\xc2\xa0mph (65\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1005\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Late on October\xc2\xa024, the NHC began to monitor the formation of an area of low pressure located south of eastern Central America.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158">\n        <a href="#cite_note-158">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system quickly gained organization as it moved northwestwards,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">\n        <a href="#cite_note-159">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and was declared Tropical Storm Selma at 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa027.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SelmaD1_160-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SelmaD1-160">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This marked only the second time that an Eastern Pacific tropical cyclone became a tropical storm east of 90\xc2\xb0W, the other being\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Alma" title="Tropical Storm Alma">\n        Alma of 2008\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SelmaD1_160-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SelmaD1-160">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With the environment thought to be generally conducive to intensification, Selma was forecast to gain some strength before moving northwards into Central America. However, with wind shear stronger than expected,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">\n        <a href="#cite_note-161">\n         [159]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       this did not materialize, and Selma never strengthened beyond minimal tropical storm status.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">\n        <a href="#cite_note-162">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eventually, at 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa028, Selma made landfall just southeast of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Salvador,_El_Salvador" title="San Salvador, El Salvador">\n        San Salvador, El Salvador\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       becoming the first Eastern Pacific tropical cyclone to make landfall anywhere in\n       <a href="/wiki/El_Salvador" title="El Salvador">\n        El Salvador\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">\n        <a href="#cite_note-164">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Once over land, Selma weakened quickly, and degenerated into a post-tropical cyclone by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa028.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">\n        <a href="#cite_note-165">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">\n        Storm names\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Storm names">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main articles:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        Tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_tropical_cyclone_naming" title="History of tropical cyclone naming">\n        History of tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_historic_tropical_cyclone_names" title="List of historic tropical cyclone names">\n        List of historic tropical cyclone names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The following names will be used for named storms that form in the northeastern Pacific Ocean during 2017.\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_hurricane_names" title="List of retired Pacific hurricane names">\n        Retired names\n       </a>\n       , if any, will be announced by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       in the spring of 2018. The names not retired from this list will be used again in the 2023 season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">\n        <a href="#cite_note-166">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This same list was used in the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2011 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2011 season\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n    </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       For storms that form in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_Pacific_Hurricane_Center" title="Central Pacific Hurricane Center">\n        Central Pacific Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       \'s area of responsibility, encompassing the area between\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140 degrees west\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        International Date Line\n       </a>\n       , all names are used in a series of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_tropical_cyclone_names#Central_Pacific" title="List of tropical cyclone names">\n        four rotating lists\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167">\n        <a href="#cite_note-167">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The next four names slated for use are shown below.\n      </p>\n      <table style="width:90%;">\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Walaka\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Akoni\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Ema\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Hone\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The usage of the Atlantic storm name "Don", and the name "Hilary", in July garnered some negative attention relating to\n       <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">\n        United States President\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">\n        Donald Trump\n       </a>\n       , and former Presidential candidate\n       <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">\n        Hillary Clinton\n       </a>\n       . People also took to Twitter to poke fun at the names and both individuals, with political jokes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">\n        <a href="#cite_note-168">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_effects">\n        Season effects\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Season effects">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       This is a table of all the storms that have formed in the 2017 Pacific hurricane season. It includes their duration, names, landfall(s), denoted in parentheses, damages, and death totals. Deaths in parentheses are additional and indirect (an example of an indirect death would be a traffic accident), but were still related to that storm. Damage and deaths include totals while the storm was extratropical, a wave, or a low, and all the damage figures are in 2017 USD.\n      </p>\n      <table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:transparent;text-align:center">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="7" nowrap="nowrap">\n         <small>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-7">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           A major hurricane is a storm that ranks as Category\xc2\xa03 or higher on the\n           <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n            Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-8">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-8">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           The totals represent the sum of the squares for every (sub)tropical storm\'s intensity of over 33\xc2\xa0knots (38\xc2\xa0mph, 61\xc2\xa0km/h), divided by 10,000. Calculations are provided at\n           <a href="/wiki/Talk:2017_Pacific_hurricane_season/ACE_calcs" title="Talk:2017 Pacific hurricane season/ACE calcs">\n            Talk:2017 Pacific hurricane season/ACE calcs\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n         </li>\n        </ol>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: References">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">\n       <ol class="references">\n        <li id="cite_note-season-1">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          <b>\n           <a href="#cite_ref-season_1-0">\n            ^\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          <cite class="citation report">\n           Dorst Neal.\n           <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20101206195446/http://www.aoml.noaa.gov/hrd/tcfaq/G1.html" rel="nofollow">\n            When is hurricane season?\n           </a>\n           (Report).
